name:Aâ€dâ€eâ€lâ€iâ€nâ€eâ€wâ€aâ€nâ€g
info:2-bed Room
info:Stayed in October 2023
info:Other
info:11 Reviews
rating:4
posted:Posted October 18, 2023
msg:The hotel's decorated rooms have very good hardware facilities, including dry and wet separation Duravit sanitary ware, Hansgrohe faucet showers, and water purification faucets, which are not available in many old five-star hotels in many cities. The model is also the same as that of a five-star resort hotel, but there are still some problems: the hotel is divided into several buildings, which are allocated in the "Hua Rui Building". When checking in, I asked whether the car could be driven to the corresponding building. The answer was yes, but there was a stone ball blocking the actual building and it could not be driven in. It could only be parked in the central parking space. No manual or guidance was found, so I had to carry the luggage myself. There were still several steps at the door of the building, and the slope was too steep. It was very inconvenient to carry heavy luggage. It is recommended that it be transformed into a large gentle slope "barrier-free passage" to facilitate wheelchairs and the like. The first room was arranged to face the Chinese restaurant It's at the back of the building, the distance between buildings is too close, facing the chimney and the school (there will be noise the next morning), the decoration smell in this room is also quite strong, the hotel has prepared an air purifier but the machine makes a lot of noise, saying that I don't need to catch a flight early in the morning and need a quiet rest, so I changed to a room opposite (only the last room left). Fortunately, the room I changed to didn't face the kitchen and the school, and the decoration smell in this room was much better. I didn't notice it at night because of the dim light, but I found that it was facing the airport runway during the day... I was woken up by the sound of consecutive planes taking off at close range early in the morning. Of course, due to the geographical location of the hotel, there is a psychological expectation, which is understandable. It is still very suitable for people who need to catch a flight early in the morning... It is recommended that you should talk to the guests more when checking in, and allocate accommodation according to different situations after obtaining their understanding. Another question not about the hotel. When I came here, there was a school next to me. At 6-7 pm, students could finish school until 8 pm. There were cars parked around to pick up students. The spacious main road with four lanes was squeezed into only one lane. It was very difficult to drive out of this road when doing business nearby. If you are catching a flight or in an emergency, you will be delayed... You should also be prepared and reserve more time.
